\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Load all data files}
\NormalTok{demographic\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_csv}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"/Volumes/YB\_Drive/NavAging\_Paper/data/demographic\_data.csv"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{non\_nav }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_csv}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"/Volumes/YB\_Drive/NavAging\_Paper/data/non\_nav\_data.csv"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{ya\_nav }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_csv}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"/Volumes/YB\_Drive/NavAging\_Paper/data/ya\_averaged\_results.csv"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{oa\_nav }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{read\_csv}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"/Volumes/YB\_Drive/NavAging\_Paper/data/oa\_averaged\_results.csv"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Combine YA and OA navigation data}
\NormalTok{nav\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{bind\_rows}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  ya\_nav }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{Group =} \StringTok{"YA"}\NormalTok{),}
\NormalTok{  oa\_nav }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{Group =} \StringTok{"OA"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Average navigation metrics across all blocks for each participant}
\NormalTok{nav\_averaged }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ nav\_data }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{group\_by}\NormalTok{(Participant, Group) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{summarise}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{Mean\_Speed =} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(Speed, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{Mean\_Distance =} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(Distance, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{Mean\_Navigation\_Time =} \FunctionTok{mean}\NormalTok{(Navigation\_Time, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{),}
    \AttributeTok{.groups =} \StringTok{"drop"}
\NormalTok{  )}

\CommentTok{\# Merge all datasets}
\NormalTok{merged\_temp }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ demographic\_data }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{full\_join}\NormalTok{(non\_nav, }\AttributeTok{by =} \StringTok{"Participant"}\NormalTok{, }\AttributeTok{suffix =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"\_demo"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"\_non\_nav"}\NormalTok{)) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{Group =} \FunctionTok{coalesce}\NormalTok{(Group\_non\_nav, }
                          \FunctionTok{if\_else}\NormalTok{(Group\_demo }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"YA"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"OA"}\NormalTok{))) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{select}\NormalTok{(}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Group\_demo, }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Group\_non\_nav)}

\NormalTok{merged\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ merged\_temp }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{left\_join}\NormalTok{(nav\_averaged, }\AttributeTok{by =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Participant"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Group"}\NormalTok{))}

\CommentTok{\# Calculate change scores}
\NormalTok{merged\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ merged\_data }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}
    \AttributeTok{SSS\_Diff =}\NormalTok{ SSS\_Post }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ SSS\_Pre,}
    \AttributeTok{SSQ\_Diff =}\NormalTok{ SSQ\_Post }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ SSQ\_Pre}
\NormalTok{  )}

\CommentTok{\# CREATE THREE{-}GROUP VARIABLE}
\CommentTok{\# Define your criteria for splitting OA into High and Low}
\CommentTok{\# Example: Split by median NARA score (or your preferred measure)}
\NormalTok{oa\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ merged\_data }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(Group }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"OA"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{nara\_median }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{median}\NormalTok{(oa\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{NARA, }\AttributeTok{na.rm =} \ConstantTok{TRUE}\NormalTok{)}

\NormalTok{merged\_data }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ merged\_data }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{mutate}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{Group\_3Level =} \FunctionTok{case\_when}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{    Group }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"YA"} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"YA"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{    Group }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"OA"} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ NARA }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=}\NormalTok{ nara\_median }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"OA\_High"}\NormalTok{,}
\NormalTok{    Group }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"OA"} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ NARA }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}}\NormalTok{ nara\_median }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \StringTok{"OA\_Low"}\NormalTok{,}
    \ConstantTok{TRUE} \SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}} \ConstantTok{NA\_character\_}
\NormalTok{  ))}

\CommentTok{\# Convert to factor with proper ordering}
\NormalTok{merged\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Group\_3Level }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(merged\_data}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Group\_3Level, }
                                    \AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"YA"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"OA\_High"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"OA\_Low"}\NormalTok{))}

\CommentTok{\# Display sample of merged data}
\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Total participants:"}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(merged\_data), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}

## Normality Tests (Shapiro-Wilk):
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\ControlFlowTok{for}\NormalTok{(grp }\ControlFlowTok{in} \FunctionTok{levels}\NormalTok{(vg\_data\_clean}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Group\_3Level)) \{}
\NormalTok{  data\_subset }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ vg\_data\_clean }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(Group\_3Level }\SpecialCharTok{==}\NormalTok{ grp) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} 
    \FunctionTok{pull}\NormalTok{(Video\_Game\_Experience\_Quantified)}
\NormalTok{  shapiro\_result }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{shapiro.test}\NormalTok{(data\_subset)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(grp, }\StringTok{": W ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(shapiro\_result}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic, }\DecValTok{4}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{", p ="}\NormalTok{, shapiro\_result}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value)}
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(shapiro\_result}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.05}\NormalTok{) }\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{" (non{-}normal)"}\NormalTok{) }\ControlFlowTok{else} \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{" (normal)"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

## OA_Low : W = 0.4227 , p = 8.898791e-07 (non-normal)
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Check homogeneity of variance}

  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"F ="}\NormalTok{, welch\_anova}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{statistic, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"df1 ="}\NormalTok{, welch\_anova}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{parameter[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{", df2 ="}\NormalTok{, welch\_anova}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{parameter[}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{], }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"p{-}value ="}\NormalTok{, welch\_anova}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value, }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  p\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ welch\_anova}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{p.value}
  
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(p\_value }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.05}\NormalTok{) \{}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Post{-}hoc Comparisons (Games{-}Howell):}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    games\_howell }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{games\_howell\_test}\NormalTok{(exercise\_data\_clean, }
\NormalTok{                                      Exercise\_Quantified }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ Group\_3Level)}
    \FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(games\_howell)}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
  
\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else}\NormalTok{ \{}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Assumptions met. Using standard one{-}way ANOVA.}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  anova\_model }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{aov}\NormalTok{(Exercise\_Quantified }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ Group\_3Level, }\AttributeTok{data =}\NormalTok{ exercise\_data\_clean)}
\NormalTok{  anova\_summary }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{summary}\NormalTok{(anova\_model)}
  
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"One{-}way ANOVA Results:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(anova\_summary)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  eta\_sq }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ effectsize}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{eta\_squared}\NormalTok{(anova\_model)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Eta{-}squared ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(eta\_sq}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Eta2[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  p\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ anova\_summary[[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]]}\SpecialCharTok{$}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{Pr(\textgreater{}F)}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
  
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(p\_value }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.05}\NormalTok{) \{}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Post{-}hoc Comparisons (Tukey HSD):}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}

    \FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(tukey\_results)}

\NormalTok{  \}}
\NormalTok{\}}

\NormalTok{  anova\_model }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{aov}\NormalTok{(Trails\_B\_CT }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ Group\_3Level, }\AttributeTok{data =}\NormalTok{ trails\_b\_clean)}
\NormalTok{  anova\_summary }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{summary}\NormalTok{(anova\_model)}
  
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"One{-}way ANOVA Results:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(anova\_summary)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  eta\_sq }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ effectsize}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{eta\_squared}\NormalTok{(anova\_model)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Eta{-}squared ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(eta\_sq}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Eta2[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  p\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ anova\_summary[[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]]}\SpecialCharTok{$}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{Pr(\textgreater{}F)}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
  
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(p\_value }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.05}\NormalTok{) \{}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Post{-}hoc Comparisons (Tukey HSD):}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    tukey\_results }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{TukeyHSD}\NormalTok{(anova\_model)}
    \FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(tukey\_results)}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}

\NormalTok{\} }\ControlFlowTok{else} \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(use\_welch) \{}

\NormalTok{  anova\_model }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{aov}\NormalTok{(SSQ\_Post }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ Group\_3Level, }\AttributeTok{data =}\NormalTok{ ssq\_post\_clean)}
\NormalTok{  anova\_summary }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{summary}\NormalTok{(anova\_model)}
  
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"One{-}way ANOVA Results:}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  \FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(anova\_summary)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  eta\_sq }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ effectsize}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{eta\_squared}\NormalTok{(anova\_model)}
  \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Eta{-}squared ="}\NormalTok{, }\FunctionTok{round}\NormalTok{(eta\_sq}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Eta2[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{], }\DecValTok{3}\NormalTok{), }\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
  
\NormalTok{  p\_value }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ anova\_summary[[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]]}\SpecialCharTok{$}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\AttributeTok{Pr(\textgreater{}F)}\StringTok{\textasciigrave{}}\NormalTok{[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{]}
  
  \ControlFlowTok{if}\NormalTok{(p\_value }\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}} \FloatTok{0.05}\NormalTok{) \{}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"Post{-}hoc Comparisons (Tukey HSD):}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{    tukey\_results }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{TukeyHSD}\NormalTok{(anova\_model)}
    \FunctionTok{print}\NormalTok{(tukey\_results)}
    \FunctionTok{cat}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"}\SpecialCharTok{\textbackslash{}n}\StringTok{"}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{  \}}
\NormalTok{\}}
\end{Highlighting}
